instruction is not counted.

<details>

Tier 1 instructions executed.

<td align="right">59.6%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">
Not specialized

<summary>ⓘ</summary>

</details>
</td>
<td align="right">3,247,590,443</td>
<td align="right">3.2%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">
Specialized hits

</tr>
